Why is it important to scroll through the planes?  The scrolling feature of this software is unique for pinpointing structures and understanding relationships of structures to one another. This unique feature actually helps you pinpoint the structure on the 3D cadaver and works whether the cadaver is whole or sectioned, for better visualization.
